<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 5.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="perfgraph"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">IX. STOCKHOLDER RETURN PERFORMANCE GRAPH</font></b></a></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 5.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following graph compares the five-year cumulative
total stockholder return (including reinvestment of dividends) of the Company,
the S&amp;P 500 Index and the S&amp;P 600 Aerospace/Defense Index.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 1.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">AAR CORP.</font><br>
Comparison of Cumulative Five Year Total
Return</font></b><sup><font face="Times New Roman" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;">1</font></sup></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="608" height="323" src="ds3744image002.gif"></font></p>

<div style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="1" width="69" noshade color="black" align="left" style="width:51.6pt;">

</font></div>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 5.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><sup><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">1</font></sup><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;">Assumes $100 invested on June 1, 1998, and
reinvestment of dividends in the Company&#146;s Common Stock, the S&amp;P 500 Index
and the S&amp;P 600 Aerospace/Defense Index.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 5.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The S&amp;P Index is comprised of domestic industry
leaders in four major sectors:&#160;
Industrials, Financials, Utilities and Transportation, and serves as a
broad indicator of the performance of the U.S. equity market. The S&amp;P 600
Aerospace/Defense Index is comprised of smallcap companies engaged in
aerospace/defense business activities presently including:&#160; AAR CORP., Aeroflex,&nbsp;Inc., Alliant
Techsystems,&nbsp;Inc., Armor Holdings,&nbsp;Inc., Cubic Corp., Curtiss-Wright
Corp., DRS Technologies, EDO Corporation, Engineered Support Systems, Esterline
Technologies Corp., GenCorp Inc., Invision Technologies Inc., Kaman Corp.,
Mercury Computer Systems Inc., Teledyne Technologies Inc., and Triumph Group,&nbsp;Inc.
The Company&#146;s prior year peer group index is comprised of Aeroflex,&nbsp;Inc.,
Alliant Techsystems,&nbsp;Inc., Armor Holdings,&nbsp;Inc., BE Aerospace,
Curtiss-Wright Corp., DRS Technologies, EDO Corporation, Engineered Support
Systems, GenCorp Inc., Kaman Corp., Mercury Computer Systems,&nbsp;Inc., and
Triumph Group,&nbsp;Inc. Cubic Corp., Esterline Technologies Corp., Invision
Technologies,&nbsp;Inc., and Teledyne Technologies Inc. were added to, and BE
Aerospace was dropped from, the S&amp;P 600 Defense/Aerospace index during
Fiscal Year 2003.</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 5.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="audit"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">X. AUDIT INFORMATION</font></b></a></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 1.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><a name="auditcomm"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Report of Audit Committee</font></b></a></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 5.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee carries out
its responsibilities pursuant to its written charter. Among other things, the
Audit Committee oversees the Company&#146;s financial reporting process and reviews
and makes recommendations to the Board concerning the reliability and integrity
of the Company&#146;s internal controls, disclosure controls, financial reporting
process and legal compliance, and the independence and performance of the
Company&#146;s internal and independent auditors. The Company&#146;s management is
primarily responsible for the Company&#146;s financial statements and the quality
and integrity of the reporting process and systems of internal control. The
Company&#146;s independent auditors are </font></p>

<font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;">
 <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;line-height:9.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;">17</p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="black" align="center">

<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=20,EFW="2115196",CP="AAR CORP",DN="1",CHK=346721,FOLIO='17',FILE="DISK027:[03CHI4.03CHI3744.EDGAR]DS3744.CHC",USER="AGAETZ",CD='Aug 22 20:51 2003' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
</font>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 5.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">responsible for auditing the
Company&#146;s financial statements and for expressing an opinion on the conformity
of the financial statements with generally accepted accounting principles in
the United States.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In fulfilling its oversight responsibilities, the Audit
Committee has reviewed and discussed the Company&#146;s audited financial statements
for the fiscal year ended May&nbsp;31, 2003, with the Company&#146;s management and
representatives of the independent auditors. Management has represented to the
Audit Committee that the Company&#146;s financial statements were prepared in
accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States
and the independent auditors have expressed an opinion based on their audit
activity that the financial statements are in conformance with generally
accepted accounting principles in the United States. The Audit Committee is not
responsible for the determination that the Company&#146;s financial statements are
complete and accurate and in accordance with accounting principles generally
accepted in the United States (&#147;GAAP&#148;).</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee reviewed and discussed with the
independent auditors and management the overall scope and plans for the audit
and the adequacy of internal controls, and met with the independent auditors
without management present to discuss the results of their examinations, their
evaluation of the Company&#146;s internal controls, disclosure controls and the
overall quality (not just acceptability) of the Company&#146;s accounting policies
and financial reporting. The Audit Committee also discussed with the
independent auditors the matters required to be discussed by Statement on
Auditing Standards No.&nbsp;61, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Communication with Audit
Committees</font></i>, as amended, their independence from the Company and its
management, including the matters in the written disclosures furnished by the
independent auditors and required by Independence Standards Board Standard No.&nbsp;1,
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Independence Discussions with Audit Committees</font></i>,
and determined that the non-audit services provided to the Company by the
independent auditor are compatible with maintaining the auditors&#146; independence.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In reliance on its review of the audited financial
statements and the discussions referred to above and subject to the limitations
on the role and responsibilities of the Audit Committee referred to above and
in the charter, the Audit Committee recommended to the Board of Directors that
the audited financial statements be included in the Company&#146;s Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K
for the year ended May&nbsp;31, 2003, for filing with the Securities and
Exchange Commission.</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Audit Committee</font></b></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A. Robert Abboud, Chairman<br>
James G. Brocksmith,&nbsp;Jr.<br>
James E. Goodwin<br>
Joel D. Spungin</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><a name="indaudit"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">INDEPENDENT AUDITORS</font></b></a></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KPMG LLP was engaged as the Company&#146;s independent
auditors for Fiscal 2003 principally to perform the annual audit and to render
certain other services.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee of the Company&#146;s Board of Directors,
after consideration and determination of the independent auditors&#146; independence
in light of all services rendered to the Company, selected KPMG LLP as its
independent auditors for the fiscal year ending May&nbsp;31, 2004. Representatives
of that firm are expected to be present at the Annual Meeting, with the
opportunity to make a statement if they so desire and to be available to
respond to appropriate questions.</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><a name="auditfees"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Audit Fees</font></b></a></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s independent auditor reports to, and is
engaged at the direction of, the Audit Committee, with approval by the Board of
Directors. Audit Committee pre-approval is required for any non-audit and audit
related services to be provided by the independent auditors in excess of
$100,000 in the aggregate.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following table sets forth the aggregate fees billed
by KPMG to the Company for Fiscal Years 2003 and 2002 for audit, audit related,
tax, and other services provided by the Company&#146;s independent auditors:</font></p>

<font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;">

  <p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">749,600</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="16" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt 0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:12.0pt;">
  <p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>

<div style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="1" width="69" noshade color="black" align="left" style="width:51.6pt;">

</font></div>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><sup><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></sup><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Audit
related fees include benefit plan audits, SEC Comment Letter review and due
diligence assistance.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><sup><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></sup><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Tax
fees include federal tax return reviews.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><sup><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></sup><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
other fees include information technology controls review and summer intern
training.</p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="other"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">XI. OTHER MATTERS TO BE
VOTED UPON</font></b></a></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management knows of no other matters which are to be
brought before the Annual Meeting. However, if any other matters properly come
before the Annual Meeting, the named proxy holders will vote all proxies in
their discretion and best judgment on such other matters.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="stockprop"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">XII. STOCKHOLDER
PROPOSALS</font></b></a><br>
FOR THE YEAR 2004 ANNUAL MEETING</p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Any
stockholder who wishes to present a proposal for consideration at the Annual
Meeting of Stockholders to be held in 2004 must submit such proposal in
accordance with the rules&nbsp;promulgated by the Securities and Exchange
Commission. Under the Company&#146;s By-Laws, in order for a proposal to be eligible
for action by the stockholders at and inclusion in the Company&#146;s proxy
statement and form of proxy relating to the 2004 Annual Meeting, the
stockholder must submit such proposal to the Company, in writing, to be
received by the Secretary of the Company, AAR CORP., One AAR Place, 1100 N.
Wood Dale Road, Wood Dale, Illinois 60191, no later than April&nbsp;11, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A stockholder proposal submitted outside Rule&nbsp;14a-8
under the Exchange Act for presentation at the 2003 Annual Meeting will be
considered untimely for purposes of Rules&nbsp;14a-4 and 14a-5 under the
Exchange Act if notice of the stockholder proposal is received by the Company
after April&nbsp;11, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 24.0pt 228.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">By Order
of the Board of Directors</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 228.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Howard A. Pulsifer<br>
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Secretary</font></i></font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">August&nbsp;27, 2003</font></p>

<p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">UPON THE
WRITTEN REQUEST OF ANY RECORD HOLDER OR BENEFICIAL OWNER OF COMMON STOCK OF AAR
CORP., THE COMPANY WILL PROVIDE, WITHOUT CHARGE, A COPY OF ITS ANNUAL REPORT ON
FORM&nbsp;l0-K FILED WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION FOR THE FISCAL
YEAR ENDED MAY&nbsp;31, 2003. REQUESTS SHOULD BE MADE TO MR. HOWARD A.
PULSIFER, SECRETARY, AAR CORP., ONE AAR PLACE, 1100 N. WOOD DALE ROAD, WOOD
DALE, ILLINOIS 60191, (630) 227-2000.</font></b></p>

<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=22,EFW="2115196",CP="AAR CORP",DN="1",CHK=923208,FOLIO='19',FILE="DISK027:[03CHI4.03CHI3744.EDGAR]DS3744.CHC",USER="AGAETZ",CD='Aug 22 20:51 2003' -->



<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:right;"><a name="appendix1"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">APPENDIX 1</font></b></a></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">AAR CORP.<br>
Board of Directors<br>
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Audit Committee Charter</font></i></font></b></p>

<p style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Purpose</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 8.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee is
appointed by the Board to assist the Board in fulfilling its oversight
responsibilities relating to (i)&nbsp;corporate accounting, disclosure and
reporting practices and legal and regulatory compliance of the Company, (ii)&nbsp;the
quality and integrity of the Company&#146;s financial statements and (iii)&nbsp;the
qualifications, independence and performance of the Company&#146;s internal audit
function and independent auditors.</font></p>

<p style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Organization</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 8.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee shall be
comprised of not less than three directors of the Company who shall meet the
compensation, independence, experience, financial expertise, and other
requirements of the New York Stock Exchange and applicable federal and state
securities law and regulations. The members of the Audit Committee shall be
appointed by the Board from time to time after considering the recommendation
of the Nominating&nbsp;&amp; Governance Committee and upon a determination by
the Board that the nominees meet all required qualifications for Audit
Committee membership.</font></p>

<p style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Committee Authority and Responsibilities</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee will maintain flexible policies
and procedures and meeting schedules, consistent with the requirements of this
Charter and the Company&#146;s by-laws, to enable the Audit Committee to best react
to changing circumstances and provide that the Company&#146;s accounting, disclosure
and reporting practices are in accordance with applicable legal and regulatory
requirements. The Chairman of the Audit Committee may call meetings during the
year as necessary, but shall call a meeting at least once each fiscal quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Committee will provide for free and open
communication between the Committee and the Company&#146;s directors, independent
auditors, internal auditors and management.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Both the Company&#146;s internal auditors and independent
auditor are ultimately accountable to the Board of Directors and the Audit
Committee as representatives of the Company&#146;s shareholders.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee, in its capacity as a committee of
the Board of Directors, shall be directly responsible for the appointment,
compensation and oversight of the work (including resolution of disagreements
between management and the auditor regarding financial reporting) of the
Company&#146;s independent auditors for the purpose of preparing or issuing an audit
report or related work. The Audit Committee shall have sole responsibility for
engaging or terminating the relation-ship with the Company&#146;s independent
auditors and the independent auditors shall report directly to the Audit
Committee. The Company shall provide appropriate funding, as determined by the
Audit Committee, for payment of compensation fees and expenses to the
independent auditor for the purpose of rendering an audit report.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee has authority to retain special
legal, accounting or other consultants to advise the Audit Committee as they
may determine appropriate. The Audit Committee may require any officer or
employee of the Company or the Company&#146;s legal counsel or independent auditor
to attend committee meetings or to meet with any members of, or consultants to,
the Audit Committee. The Company shall provide for appropriate funding, as
determined by the Audit Committee, in its capacity as a committee of the Board
of Directors, for payment of all fees and expenses to any advisors employed by
the Audit Committee pursuant to its authority under this Charter or applicable
law or regulations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee shall establish procedures for the
receipt, retention and treatment of complaints received by the Company
regarding accounting, internal accounting controls or auditing </font></p>

<font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;">
 <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;line-height:9.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A-</font>1</p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="black" align="center">

<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=23,EFW="2115196",CP="AAR CORP",DN="1",CHK=111930,FOLIO='A-1',FILE="DISK027:[03CHI4.03CHI3744.EDGAR]DU3744.CHC",USER="AGAETZ",CD='Aug 11 16:25 2003' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
</font>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">matters, as well as the confidential, anonymous
submissions by employees of the Company of concerns regarding questionable
accounting or auditing matters.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 8.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Audit Committee shall make
regular reports to the Board.</font></p>

<p style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt 10.1pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">In
carrying out its duties and responsibilities, the Audit Committee shall:</font></i></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Review and assess
the adequacy of the Audit Committee charter annually and submit any recommended
changes to the Board for approval.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Approve and
recommend to the Board for appointment and engage independent auditors that
meet NYSE and applicable securities law and regulatory requirements to audit
the financial statements of the Company and its divisions and subsidiaries and
the Company&#146;s pension plans.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Review written
statements from the independent auditors delineating all non-audit
relationships between the independent auditors and the Company, review with the
independent auditors the effect of any disclosed relationships or services on
objectivity and independence of the independent auditors, take appropriate
action to ensure the independence of the appointed independent auditors and
approve the compensation arrangements and proxy statement disclosures of compensation,
fees and expenses paid to independent auditors.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Receive and
review, at least annually, a report by the independent auditors describing (i)&nbsp;the
auditors internal quality control procedures and (ii)&nbsp;any material issues
raised by the most recent internal quality control review of peer group review
of the firm or by governmental or professional authorities in the preceding
five years relating to an independent audit conducted by the firm and
resolution of such issues.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Approve in
advance, as a Committee of the whole or by delegation of authority to one or
more members of the Committee, any permitted non-audit services performed by
the Company&#146;s independent auditor, including tax services, and cause such
approval to be disclosed in the Company&#146;s periodic filings as required by
applicable regulations.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Discuss with the
independent auditors the matters required to be discussed by Statement on
Auditing Standards No.&nbsp;61 and other applicable laws and regulatory
requirements relating to the conduct of the audit.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Meet with the
independent auditors and financial management of the Company to review the
scope of the proposed audit for the upcoming year and the audit procedures to
be used; at the conclusion of the year review such audit, including any comments
or recommendations of the independent auditors.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Review with the
Company&#146;s independent auditors, internal auditors, and financial and accounting
personnel, the adequacy and effectiveness of the internal controls and
disclosure controls of the Company, and elicit any recommendations for the
improvement of such internal control and disclosure control procedures or
particular areas where new or more detailed controls or procedures are
desirable.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Review the
internal audit function of the Company, including its organizational structure,
authority and independence of reporting obligations, department budget,
qualification of personnel and the proposed audit plans for the coming year,
and the coordination of such plans with the outside auditors. Review and concur
with the appointment, reassignment or dismissal of the Director of Internal
Audit.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Receive, review and
discuss with the Company&#146;s independent auditors, and internal auditor as
appropriate (i)&nbsp;a summary of significant findings from completed internal
audits, together with management&#146;s response, and periodic progress reports,
with explanation for any deviations from the original plan; (ii)&nbsp;all
critical accounting policies and practices to be used; (iii)&nbsp;all
alternative treatments of financial information within GAAP (generally accepted
accounting </p>

<font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;">
 <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;line-height:9.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A-</font>2</p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="black" align="center">

<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=24,EFW="2115196",CP="AAR CORP",DN="1",CHK=286773,FOLIO='A-2',FILE="DISK027:[03CHI4.03CHI3744.EDGAR]DU3744.CHC",USER="AGAETZ",CD='Aug 11 16:25 2003' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
</font>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">principles) that have been
discussed with management, (iv)&nbsp;ramifications of alternative disclosures
and treatments, and the treatment preferred by the auditor; and (v)&nbsp;other
material written communications between the independent auditor and management.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Review and discuss (i)&nbsp;significant
financial risks, (ii)&nbsp;the financial statements, and (iii)&nbsp;the Company&#146;s
draft MD&amp;A for the period with management and the independent auditors,
prior to issuance of an earnings release or earnings guidance or their filing
or distribution to shareholders. Among the items to be discussed are (i)&nbsp;accounting
principles, practices and judgments, (ii)&nbsp;whether the independent auditors
are satisfied with the disclosure and content of the financial statements to be
presented to the shareholders, and (iii)&nbsp;any changes in accounting
principles.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Provide sufficient
opportunity for the Committee to meet separately in executive session each
quarter with (i)&nbsp;management, (ii)&nbsp;the independent auditors, and (iii)&nbsp;the
internal auditor. Among the items to be discussed in these meetings are the
auditors&#146; evaluation of the Company&#146;s financial, accounting, and auditing
personnel, the auditors&#146; judgments about the Company&#146;s accounting principles as
applied to its financial reporting; the level of management cooperation that
the outside auditors received during the course of the audit; and management&#146;s
assessment of the performance of the auditors.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Review the human
resources and succession planning of the accounting and financial operations
within the Company.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">14.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Receive reports
concerning the Company&#146;s Assist Line activity and any non-compliance with the
Company&#146;s Code of Business Conduct and Ethics by any officers of the Company
and approve any waivers therefrom and any &#147;related party&#148; transactions.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">15.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Report on significant
matters discussed at each Committee meeting to the Board.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">16.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Investigate, as
appropriate, any matter brought to its attention within the scope of its
duties, with the power to retain outside counsel or a second independent
accountant, at the expense of the Company, for this purpose if, in its
judgment, that is appropriate.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">17.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Prepare an appropriate
Audit Committee report to shareholders to be included in the Company&#146;s annual
proxy statement that is consistent with applicable law and Securities and
Exchange Commission requirements.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;text-indent:-20.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">18.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Perform any other
activities consistent with this Charter, the Company&#146;s by-laws, and governing
law and regulations, as the Committee or Board deems necessary or appropriate.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While the Audit Committee has the responsibilities and
powers set forth in this Charter, it is not the duty of the Audit Committee to
prepare financial statements, plan or conduct audits or to determine that the
Company&#146;s financial statements are complete and accurate and are in accordance
with generally accepted accounting principles and applicable rules&nbsp;and
regulations. These are the responsibility of management and the Company&#146;s
independent auditor.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;">Dear
Stockholder:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;">We encourage you
to submit your proxy for the voting of your shares electronically this year
either by telephone or the Internet. This will eliminate the need to return
your proxy card. You will need your proxy card and Social Security Number
(where applicable) when voting your shares electronically. The Voter Control
Number that appears on the reverse side of this card, must be used in order to
submit your proxy vote by telephone or the Internet.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;">The EquiServe
Vote by Telephone and Vote by Internet systems can be accessed 24-hours a day,
seven days a week until the day prior to the meeting.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:9.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;"><b><u><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-weight:bold;">To submit your proxy vote by
Telephone:</font></u></b><br>
Using a touch-tone phone call toll-free: 1-877-PRX-VOTE/1-877-779-8683</p>

<p style="font-size:9.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt 20.15pt;"><b><u><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-weight:bold;">To submit your proxy vote by
Internet:</font></u></b><br>
Log onto the Internet and go to the website: http://www.eproxyvote.com/air</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><i><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-style:italic;">Note:
If you submit your proxy over the Internet, you may incur costs such as <br>
telecommunication and Internet access charges for which you will be
responsible.</font></i></p>

<p align="center" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 6.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;">THANK YOU FOR
VOTING YOUR SHARES<br>
YOUR VOTE IS IMPORTANT!</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 2.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><b><i><font size="1" face="Helvetica" style="font-size:9.0pt;">Do not return
this Proxy Card if you are submitting your proxy by telephone or the Internet</font></i></b></p>
